hui	Ogoni hondowa hale halu hewaria Ngode Datagaliwabenaga anda
hui	biagoha howa dahuliyali kariali biaruhondo bi mbira dalimuore
hui	layuago hale haru. Hale halu hewaria ogodagua layua. Ngode
hui	Datagaliwabenaga keba holene ndisi be kariaha ngaru dindini
hui	odope hole pudaba, lalu layuago hale haru.
hui	Kini kariali biaru aria duriali homai ho halu waraganego haru
hui	kago kanego ibu áyu nahego mani holebira. Mani ibu harangi
hui	ibugua tigi mbira hangu haru holebira.
hui	Ani bidagonaga irame Babilono dai holebira,
hui	Ibunaga de ira hungu ale howa ibunaga haguaneni haru haga manda
hui	dewa bu heneya. Ibuni mini mbira gilibu wiago ogoninaga irane
hui	ogo aledalo mbiralime manda bibe nahe ibuni hangume manda bida.
hui	Ani buleberogo wayali hararume bibahende i̱ha howa mo
hui	yulebirago ogo. Tinaga Ngode Datagaliwabe i̱ halu tibi nde
hui	i̱naga waneigini holebira.
hui	Ani lowa ibugua la dege bialu lalu, Mbuga ogoniha mani
hui	bulebiragonaga bi lo ngaru bulene horo kaware harago wia do
